			var oldonload = window.onload;
			if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
				window.onload = func;
			} else {
				window.onload = function () {

		<header class="entry-header">
			<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://off-guardian.org/2018/03/16/uks-novichok-claim-exposed-as-lies-what-is-the-current-reality-of-the-skripal-case/" rel="bookmark">UPDATED: UK’s “novichok” claim exposed as lies: what is the current reality of the Skripal&nbsp;case?</a></h2>		</header>
		<div class="story">
			<div class="entry-author">
				<span>by</span> <a href="https://off-guardian.org/author/admin1offg/" title="Posts by Admin" rel="author">Admin</a>			</div><!-- end .entry-author -->
			<p class="summary">Clearly we currently are in no position to know what really happened to the Skripals, how it happened, where it happened or who was responsible.  Just as clearly the government and media are lying. In addition the media are trying to work up a jingoistic anti-Russia hysteria that has no parallel in recent times. Not even the 2003 media frenzy to get pubic opinion behind the illegal war on Iraq reached these heights.</p>

		</aside><aside id="zuki_recentposts_medium-23" class="widget widget_zuki_recentposts_medium">
		<h3 class="widget-title">media fakery?</h3>

	</aside><aside id="text-47" class="widget widget_text">			<div class="textwidget"><h6><a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/deconstructingISIS">more posts in this category</a></h6></div>
		</aside></div><!-- #front-fullwidth-top --><div id="front-content-two" class="front-content widget-area">
	<aside id="text-22" class="widget widget_text">			<div class="textwidget"><h3> your feedback...</h3>

<blockquote class="comment"> 
We fattened feeder pigs into market hogs on the farm. When the pigs were weaned, we had to make noise and call for them when feeding time rolled around so they’d know it was time to get fed.

It didn’t take long before they associated the sound of the metal bucket scooping up corn with feeding time, and we no longer had to call the pigs, they came running, mouths open and hungry for slop.

That’s what I see when turning on CNN or FOX or MSNBC, etc. People are so well-programmed, that when they turn the Boob Tube to those channels, they sit on the couch, mouth wide open, expecting news, but all they get is slop..<cite> Greg Bacon  on  <a href="https://off-guardian.org/2017/03/15/letters-to-editor-of-europhysics-news-follow-up-to-jones-et-al/#comment-60389">”is Europhysics News announcing it will censor science papers on political grounds?" </a></cite>
</blockquote>

<blockquote class="comment">When wealth and the power it brings to bear can influence the viability of a scientists future it also leads to the inescapable logic that in too many cases, the scientist who toes the political and scientific “line” of concordance will ultimately be awarded a future while those who question or offer science in contradiction can be silenced. This is a worrying development in the war on information
<cite>Mohandeer  on <a href="https://off-guardian.org/2017/03/15/letters-to-editor-of-europhysics-news-follow-up-to-jones-et-al/comment-page-1/#comment-60323">is Europhysics News announcing it will censor science papers on political grounds?" </a></cite>
</blockquote></div>

				 <h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://off-guardian.org/2018/01/20/mark-curtis-launches-declassified/" rel="bookmark">Mark Curtis launches “Declassified&#8221;</a></h2>				 <div class="entry-author">

				<p class="summary">Mark Curtis writes I am about to publish on this site hundreds of UK declassified documents and articles on British foreign policy towards various countries. This will be the first time such a collection has been brought together online. The declassified documents, mainly from the UK’s National Archives, reveal British policy-makers actual concerns and priorities from the 1940s until the present day, from the...</p>
				<div class="entry-date"><a href="https://off-guardian.org/2018/01/20/mark-curtis-launches-declassified/" class="entry-date">January 20, 2018</a></div>
								<div class="entry-comments">
					<a href="https://off-guardian.org/2018/01/20/mark-curtis-launches-declassified/#comments">Comments 11</a>				</div><!-- end .entry-comments -->

					<a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/censorship/" rel="category tag">censorship</a>, <a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/free-speech2/" rel="category tag">free speech2</a>, <a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/latest/" rel="category tag">latest</a>				</div><!-- end .entry-cats -->
		</div><!--end .story -->

	</article><!-- end .post-43774 -->

				<p class="summary">The unofficial Christmas truce of 1914, year 1 of the Great War, saw German, British and French soldiers  defying orders to openly fraternise in no-man’s land and even in each other’s trenches. Gifts were exchanged, carols were sung. Peace reigned in the midst of war.  This was not to the liking of the military establishment, and the following year the artillery was...</p>

				 <a href="https://off-guardian.org/2017/12/24/dickens-christmas-carol/"><img width="883" height="715" src="https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png?w=883&amp;h=715&amp;crop=1" class="attachment-zuki-fullwidth size-zuki-fullwidth wp-post-image" alt="" srcset="https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png 883w, https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png?w=150&amp;h=121&amp;crop=1 150w, https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png?w=300&amp;h=243&amp;crop=1 300w, https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png?w=768&amp;h=622&amp;crop=1 768w" sizes="(max-width: 883px) 100vw, 883px" data-attachment-id="42896" data-permalink="https://off-guardian.org/2017/12/24/dickens-christmas-carol/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01/" data-orig-file="https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png" data-orig-size="883,715" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Screen Shot 2017-12-23 at 20.42.01" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://offgraun.files.wordpress.com/2017/12/screen-shot-2017-12-23-at-20-42-01.png?w=840" /></a>
			</div><!-- end .entry-thumb -->
			
			<div class="story">
				 <h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://off-guardian.org/2017/12/24/dickens-christmas-carol/" rel="bookmark">Dickens’ A Christmas Carol:  cosy seasonal tale or passionate condemnation of unfettered&nbsp;capitalism?</a></h2>				 <div class="entry-author">
					<span>by</span> <a href="https://off-guardian.org/author/blackcatte/" title="Posts by Catte" rel="author">Catte</a>				</div><!-- end .entry-author -->
				<p class="summary">Today we think of Charles Dickens’ A Christmas Carol as a cosy piece of traditional seasonal fare, replete with steaming puds and roasted goose and comfortably easy lessons about not being stingy at Crimbo. But when Dickens wrote his novella in 1843 he was delivering a far more serious - and possibly freshly relevant  - warning about the moral bankruptcy of a society...</p>
				<div class="entry-date"><a href="https://off-guardian.org/2017/12/24/dickens-christmas-carol/" class="entry-date">December 24, 2017</a></div>
								<div class="entry-comments">
					<a href="https://off-guardian.org/2017/12/24/dickens-christmas-carol/#comments">Comments 10</a>				</div><!-- end .entry-comments -->
								<div class="entry-cats">
					<a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/arts/" rel="category tag">Arts</a>, <a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/arts-and-entertainment/" rel="category tag">Arts and Entertainment</a>, <a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/featured/" rel="category tag">featured</a>, <a href="https://off-guardian.org/category/historical-perspectives/" rel="category tag">historical perspectives</a>				</div><!-- end .entry-cats -->
		</div><!--end .story -->
		</div><!--end .rp-big-one -->
	</article><!-- end .post-42783 -->

	 <article id="post-42955" class="rp-medium-one post-42955 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-documentaries category-latest tag-institutional-psychopathy tag-peter-coyote">

	}

</script>
</body>
</html>
